 'riktar paimaane' kaa puraa naam richter pariman pareekshan paimaana (richter magnitude test scale) he or laghu rup main ise sthanik pariman (local magnitude) he
 Why It Comes The upper surface of the earthquake is made up of seven tectonic plates
 jahaan bhi ye platen ek duusare se takaraati hai vahaan bukamp kaa khatra paidaa ho jaataa he

 Bollywood actress Katrina Kaif is as good a fitness freak as she is
 katrina kii life main fitness kii ek ahm jagah he
 Katrina believes that every person must include fitness in their life to stay fit
 haalanki duusare kii tarah shaareerik kad-lathi paane ke prayaas karne kii katrina bilkul khilaaf hai
 Katrina says that she does not believe in an 'ideal body texture' nor is there an 'ideal body texture' the way women should look
 bataa den, 'bharat' kii is abhinetri ke paas kai tarah kii patibaddhtaayen hai or vah kai-kai ghanton tak kaam karti rahati hai, lekin in sabko vah apane fitness kii raah par aane nahin detii hai
 Talking to IANS over phone, Katrina said, 'it is very easy
 ek din main 24 ghante hote hai
 If you cannot take even 40 minutes in a day, then it is up to you whether you want to or not
 yadi fitness aapke liye jaruri he to aap jahaan kahin bhi hai aap din main 45 minute jarur nikaal sakate hai
 "katrina continued," There are many such training that anyone can do
 sabase mahatvapurn baat training ke us prakaar ko dhundhana he jo aap par kaam karata ho
 Do not think about copying someone else
 "bharat main ribok kii nai brands ambesader ne bataaya ki ek mahila apni khud kii twachaa main jis tarah se sahaj mahasoos karti he use usee tarah se dikhnaa chahie, jis tarah se vah dikhnaa chaahati he or yah hamamen se sabhi ko nishchay karnaa hoga ki hamaari adarsh body kis tarah kii honi chahie jise ham fitness ke madhyam se paanaa chaahate hai
 Regarding joining Reebok, he said, "when it comes to Reebok, i think we both have the same approach to fitness

 chitt ke sambandh chalem na chalem, lekin vitt ke jarur chalate hai

 unhone kaha ki november kaa maheenaa vitt ke lihaaj se koi nahin bhul saktaa

 tip karke likhi na ki bolkar

 main kavita premi hum or unhen kavita bilkul pasand nahin

 maine kaha milakar baat karte hai
